Each set contains 2 entries.
Number of bits used for the index is 3.

Number of virtual pages is 8.
Number of physical pages is 8.
Each page contains 1024 bytes.
Number of bits used for the page table index is 3.
Number of bits used for the page offset is 10.

D-cache contains 4 sets.
Each set contains 1 entries.
Each line is 16 bytes.
The cache uses a write-allocate and write-back policy.
Number of bits used for the index is 2.
Number of bits used for the offset is 4.

L2-cache contains 16 sets.
Each set contains 4 entries.
Each line is 16 bytes.
The cache uses a no write-allocate and write-through policy.
Number of bits used for the index is 4.
Number of bits used for the offset is 4.

The addresses read in are virtual addresses.
L2 cache is disabled in this configuration.
